<a href="/market">Market Charts</a> > <a href="/market/2016/summary">2016</a> > Movie Chart

<h1>Annual Movie Chart - 2016</h1>
<div>
<span class="alignleft"><a href="/market/2015/top-grossing-movies">&larr; 2015</a></span><span class="alignright"><a href="/market/2017/top-grossing-movies">2017 &rarr;</a></span>
</div>
<div class="clearfloats"></div>

<p><B>Note:</B> This chart ranks movies by the amount they earned during 2016.
It includes movies released in previous years that earned money during 2016.
For example, a movie released over Thanksgiving in 2015 will most likely earn money in 2015 and 2016.
Click on the individual movie to see its total gross over all the years in which it played.
<p>Each box office year ends on the first Sunday of the following year.
The next year starts the following day (Monday).
For example, the "2004 box office year" ended on Sunday, January 2, 2005.
<P>Inflation-adjusted figures are based on ticket sale estimates.

<P>See <a href="/box-office-records/domestic/all-movies/cumulative/released-in-2016">Top 2016 Movies at the Domestic Box Office</a> for the total domestic box office for the top 100 movies released in 2016.
